          <div class="Pos-r Z-0 article-container legacy" data-template="desktop" id="article--walking-dead--fan-pulls-zombie-prank-on-norman-reedus--watch-him-scream-175823835" style="background-color:white;min-height:315px;">
           <div class="Pos-r sticky-container print-article" style="min-height:315px;">
            <div class="article-inner-container" style="max-width:1280px;">
             <div class="inset-container Mx-a">
              <div class="GridTable">
               <div class="D-tbr row-template">
                <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t col-left">
                 <div class="content" style="width:825px;min-width:825px;">
                  <noscript>
                  </noscript>
                  <noscript>
                  </noscript>
                  <div class="GridTable grid-content">
                   <div class="D-tbr row-content">
                    <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t col-left Pend-20" style="width:305px;max-width:305px;">
                     <h1 class="Font-A-6-110 title W-100" id="article-aft-title--walking-dead--fan-pulls-zombie-prank-on-norman-reedus--watch-him-scream-175823835">
                      'Walking Dead' Superfan Pulls Zombie Prank on Norman Reedus: See Daryl Dixon Scream!
                     </h1>
                     <div class="attribution-component D-b W-100" id="article-aft-attribution--walking-dead--fan-pulls-zombie-prank-on-norman-reedus--watch-him-scream-175823835" style="max-width:305px;">
                      <div class="author-info author-info-text-first Pt-10 W-100 Bd-t Bd-b Bdstart-0 Bdend-0">
                       <div class="GridTable W-100">
                        <div class="D-tbr">
                         <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t provider-info">
                          <div class="provider-alias C-n">
                           <span class="Font-C-2-140 Fw-b">
                            Yahoo TV
                           </span>
                          </div>
                         </div>
                        </div>
                       </div>
                       <div class="GridTable W-100">
                        <div class="D-tbr">
                         <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t">
                          <cite class="byline col D-b Fs-n" style="padding-bottom:15px;">
                           <time class="date Font-C-2-140 Fw-n D-b">
                            <span>
                             January 17, 2014
                            </span>
                           </time>
                          </cite>
                         </div>
                        </div>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t col-right" style="max-width:500px;">
                     <div class="text-body-wrapper W-100 Font-B-1-160">
                      <noscript>
                      </noscript>
                      <div class="text-body W-100 Font-B-1-160" id="article-aft-text-body--walking-dead--fan-pulls-zombie-prank-on-norman-reedus--watch-him-scream-175823835" style="color:#222222;max-width:500px;">
                       <div class="body read-more-cut">
                        <div class="pre-cut" style="height:auto;margin-bottom:1.5em;">
                         <p>
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:15df256c-f322-32a6-aecf-70442b626721;t9:18;itc:0" href="https://s.yimg.com/os/publish-images/tv/2014-01-17/66528355-6eec-4135-be05-07b65ea42aff_norman-reedus-walking-dead-zombie-prank.jpg" target="_blank">
                           <div>
                            <img align="middle" alt="'Walking Dead' Superfan Pulls Zombie Prank on Norman Reedus: See Daryl Dixon Scream!" class="editorial" src="https://s.yimg.com/lo/api/res/1.2/5LD9SbCb0o3Y_WRT5w3CXg--/YXBwaWQ9bWFnYXppbmVzO3c9ODAw/https://s.yimg.com/os/publish-images/tv/2014-01-17/66528355-6eec-4135-be05-07b65ea42aff_norman-reedus-walking-dead-zombie-prank.jpg" title="" width="800"/>
                            <p class="legend">
                            </p>
                           </div>
                          </a>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          As "The Walking Dead" hero Daryl Dixon, he's seen the most gruesome zombie kills  and been on the operator end of several of them with his trusty bow and arrows  but that doesn't make Norman Reedus immune to getting the bejeezus scared out of him when a zombie jumps out at him in his hotel room.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          The "zombie" in question is "TWD" superfan Nick Santonastasso, who, along with "TWD" star Andrew Lincoln and producer Greg Nicotero, got a scream out of Reedus in the video, when Santonastasso jumped out of a hotel room service cart and startled Reedus.
                         </p>
                         <span>
                          <div class="yom-figure yom-fig-center" id="ymh-player-swf" style="left:0px;">
                           <iframe allowfullscreen="" class="embed-module" data-embed-type="embedIframes" data-src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/igDzM4CyWa8" frameborder="0" height="354" id="embed-video-dialog170" width="630">
                           </iframe>
                          </div>
                         </span>
                         <p>
                          Nicotero, also the series' visual effects whiz, put his best zombie makeup on Santonastasso, a New Jersey teen who documents his video pranks on his popular
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:15df256c-f322-32a6-aecf-70442b626721;t9:18;itc:0" href="https://vine.co/Nick.Santonastasso" target="_blank">
                           Vine page
                          </a>
                          , which has more than a half a million followers. Santonastasso, 17, was born with a rare syndrome called Hanhart, and has only one arm and no legs, but, as his
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:15df256c-f322-32a6-aecf-70442b626721;t9:18;itc:0" href="https://twitter.com/nicksanto534" target="_blank">
                           Twitter
                          </a>
                          tagline proclaims, lives by the motto "No excuses."
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          The impressive teen was flown to Japan, where Reedus, Lincoln, and Nicotero are promoting the second half of the series' fourth season, which premieres on Feb. 9 on AMC.
                         </p>
                         <p>

                         <p>
                          Santonastasso also tweeted a photo of himself with his new pals Reedus and Lincoln, post-prank.

src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F275a28c12e715a6bbf38cf8e3bf818b2819a0e03.jpg\" alt=\"&apos;Sex&amp;Drugs&amp;Rock&amp;Roll&apos;: Can Denis Leary Become A Rock Star?\" width=\"540\" height=\"360\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EI&#x2019;m pretty sure Denis Leary did not intend his new show \u003Ci\u003ESex&amp;Drugs&amp;Rock&amp;Roll\u003C\u002Fi\u003E to be interpreted this way, but, hey, rock &amp; roll makes up its rules as it goes along: This FX series premiering Thursday makes a very good case for the notion that there&#x2019;s no such thing as authenticity in rock music.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ENever one to go for subtlety, Leary stars as a musician named Johnny Rock, a 50 year-old cult star who, we&#x2019;re supposed to believe, could have been a big star if only he hadn&#x2019;t feuded with the Keith Richards to his Mick Jagger, his co-writer\u002Flead-guitarist Flash (John Corbett, whose achievement here is extending his wastrel-musician character from\u003Ci\u003E Parenthood\u003C\u002Fi\u003E into complete degeneracy). Johnny, who still struts around with a rooster hairdo lifted from the head of Rod Stewart circa \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.youtube.com\u002Fwatch?v=HLBFyS2hlhw\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003EGasoline Alley\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, broke up the band and has been grasping at fame for about three decades now, when his new meal ticket suddenly arrives.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThat meal ticket takes the form of his long-lost daughter, who&#x2019;s got the youth, pipes, and Instagrammed body to give anyone&#x2019;s career a boost, and if you think that sounds crude, that is exactly what show-creator Leary wants you to think when you look at and listen to Gigi. She&#x2019;s played by Elizabeth Gillies, a Broadway and Nickelodeon vet who&#x2019;s immediately convincing as a young professional with daddy issues who is not above using Johnny as cynically as he plans to use her. A warm family sitcom \u003Ci\u003ESex&amp;Drugs\u003C\u002Fi\u003E is not.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-embed tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Ciframe width=\"540\" height=\"304\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.youtube.com\u002Fembed\u002FAsmxcw4iFME?feature=oembed\"\u003E\u003C\u002Fiframe\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ENeither is it a very funny sitcom. In \u003Ci\u003ERescue Me,\u003C\u002Fi\u003E Leary had the benefit of co-creator Peter Tolan and a deep bench of talented co-stars to whom he was willing to cede the spotlight. This time around, Leary surrounds himself with good actors who are very much the actor-equivalent of a back-up band, and he crowds Gillies for the spotlight in every scene they share. This is not wise when the punchlines he gives himself include, &#x201C;I wanna blow Bruce Jenner&#x201D; and &#x201C;I&#x2019;m not writing some auto-tune Katy Perry bulls&#x2013;t.&#x201D; Maybe I&#x2019;d feel more charitable about this had Leary not co-opted the title of a \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.youtube.com\u002Fwatch?v=2TBSqS4yMrM\"\u003Egreat Ian Dury song\u003C\u002Fa\u003E and failed to make his own, self-written theme song one-thousandth as good.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EYou&#x2019;re supposed to think Johnny Rock is a jerk who&#x2019;s actually heroic because he&#x2019;s fighting for the rebel spirit of rock, but I&#x2019;ll bet there are a lot of viewers who&#x2019;ll identify more with Gigi, a realist who&#x2019;s fighting for the freedom that comes with being a pop star nowadays. In Gigi&#x2019;s cosmos &#x2014; and mine &#x2014; Katy Perry is as legit as Steven Tyler, or Jon Bon Jovi, or any other rocker the show invokes.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"335\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Ff7ccab73b890d979bdf6a5d89cb1ae18cb9fe6c8.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ETV and rock &amp; roll have a history as long as both mediums. Not just Elvis Presley wiggling from the waist-up on \u003Ci\u003EThe Ed Sullivan Show\u003C\u002Fi\u003E, but also Ricky Nelson smuggling future Presley guitarist James Burton onto the otherwise-anodyne \u003Ci\u003EThe Adventures of Ozzie and Harriet\u003C\u002Fi\u003E (1952-&#x2019;66). From \u003Ci\u003EThe Monkees\u003C\u002Fi\u003E to \u003Ci\u003EEmpire\u003C\u002Fi\u003E, television shows that use pop music as a metaphor for freedom, fame, and wealth have always been compromised projects, some better than others.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ENow that rock is merely one genre among many from which a singer like Gigi plucks a melody or tempo, the bottom-line message of \u003Ci\u003ESex&amp;Drugs&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fi\u003E&#x2014; that one kind of music is privileged with a unique truth &#x2014; is undercut by what&#x2019;s actually onscreen: the spectacle of a deluded rocker being aced by a shrewd pop-ster.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ESex&amp;Drugs&amp;Rock&amp;Roll \u003Ci\u003Eairs Thursday at 10 p.m. on FX.
